## Current Audit Read

- The intake process is working at the packaging level:
  - bounded batches
  - manifests
  - source maps
  - tension / cluster / candidate summary outputs
- Parallel outer-lane work is now real across:
  - `a2_feed_high entropy doc`
  - `upgrade docs`
  - `a2_runtime_state archived old state`
  - `sims` as a separate source class
- The current bias is still toward `SOURCE_MAP_PASS` and first-pass structural mapping on large docs.
- The strongest immediate system-useful batches are:
  - `BATCH_a2feed_branchthread_family_engine_pattern__v1`
  - `BATCH_a2feed_apple_notes_term_conflict__v1`
  - `BATCH_a2feed_grok_toe_redo_tension_map__v1`
  - `BATCH_A2MID_branchthread_workflow_repair__v1`
  - `BATCH_A2MID_apple_axis_term_conflicts__v1`
  - `BATCH_A2MID_grok_toe_quarantine_tensions__v1`
- `sims/` intake has started and remains correctly separated as its own source class:
  - `BATCH_sims_top_level_docs_source_map__v1`
- The next quality gap is no longer “did intake start?”
  - it is selective second-pass refinement and later A2-mid reduction from the strongest batches rather than continued broad source-map passes.
